====================================================================================================
13. IMPLEMENTATION REFERENCE — WHERE TO INJECT
====================================================================================================

Key injection points for feature implementation:

  SSAO/SSIL:          After deferred sun (draw 3641), before light volumes
  SSS (subsurface):   After deferred sun, needs skin material mask from GBuffer
  Shadow replacement: Replace draws [2590-3640] or intercept shadow RT bind
  RT shadows:         After GBuffer [1407-2583], before deferred lighting
  Voxel GI:           Re-render GBuffer geometry into voxel grid before deferred
  Tessellation:       Intercept GBuffer draws, add HS/DS for displacement
  Material upgrade:   Replace GBuffer PS (per source file: objects, terrain, skin, etc.)
  Bloom replacement:  Replace bloom chain draws
  Tonemapping:        Replace composite draw
  FXAA replacement:   Replace final output draws

Material source files to patch for each feature:

  Subsurface Scattering:
    - skin.hlsl (character skin)
    - character.hlsl (full character body)
    - Need to encode SSS profile ID in GBuffer (RT1.A currently has emissive/translucency)

  Better Normals:
    - objects.hlsl (all static objects)
    - terrainfp4.hlsl (terrain)
    - triplanar.hlsl (rocks/cliffs)
    - skin.hlsl, character.hlsl (characters)

  Displacement/Tessellation:
    - terrain.hlsl / terrainfp4.hlsl (add HS/DS)
    - objects.hlsl (add HS/DS for detailed objects)
    - rtwtessellator.hlsl already exists for shadow tessellation — reuse pattern

  Water Improvement:
    - water.hlsl (flow maps, reflection, scum, rain)
    - Forward pass, not in GBuffer — has own PBR lighting

  Sky Improvement:
    - SkyX_Skydome.hlsl (atmospheric scattering)
    - SkyX_Clouds.hlsl, SkyX_VolClouds.hlsl
